			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism

				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic

									value = v

								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }

							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}

						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 0 }

					}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}

				add = -10

										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }

								}

				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = EUU
					}
				}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = eurosceptic
						value = -0.1
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 1 }
					}

					}
				}

						value = 0.3
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 1 }

					has_global_flag = european_federation

				set_country_flag = focus_EU301_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU301
			}
			} #hidden_effect
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.3
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.4
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.5
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
		}

					}

					has_global_flag = european_federation
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU306_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU306
			}
			} #hidden_effect
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}

					}
					else_if = {

					else_if = {

						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 0 }
					}
			}

					}

						value = 0.20
					}

							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }

						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic < 0 }

			modifier = {
				add = 40
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1

			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU403
			}
			} #hidden_effect
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}

				add = -10

					}

									value = v

									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }

			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}

							var = eurosceptic
